     <!-- Initial js to build the banner for speed perception -->
     <script>
      (function(){
             if(document.querySelectorAll('.banner--homepage').length){
                 var banner = document.querySelectorAll('.banner--homepage')[0];
 
                 buildHomeBanner(banner);
             }
 
             function buildHomeBanner(banner){
                 var winHeight = window.innerHeight,
                     bannerCaption = document.querySelectorAll('.banner__nav')[0],
                     bannerCaptionHeight = bannerCaption.offsetHeight,
                     firstBanner = banner.querySelectorAll('.banner__slide')[0],
                     firstBannerImage = firstBanner.querySelectorAll('.banner__image')[0],
                     firstBannerImageUrl = firstBannerImage.getAttribute('data-original') + '?w=50&pg=50';
 
                 banner.style.height = (winHeight - bannerCaptionHeight) + 'px';
                 firstBanner.classList.add('banner__slide--active');
                 firstBannerImage.classList.add('banner__image--active');
 
                 firstBannerImage.style.background = 'url(' + firstBannerImageUrl + ') no-repeat ' + firstBannerImage.getAttribute('data-position');
                 firstBannerImage.style.backgroundSize = 'cover';
                 //firstBannerImage.style.filter = 'blur(25px)'
             }
         })();
     </script>

        <h2 class="content__header">
         Planning Your Trip
        </h2>
        <div class="content wrapper">
         <div class="container welcome__grid">
          <div class="container grid-split">
           <div class="background--none">
            <h3 class="centered">
             Alaska is Big
            </h3>
            <p>
             It can be overwhelming to plan a trip to Alaska. What are the best spots to see bears or moose or beautiful sunsets? Do you want to spend a lot of time in one area exploring the wilderness and mountains or make those side excursions while visiting Alaska’s diverse cities? Because Alaska is so big, it’s divided into 5 regions—start your planning by learning about these different locations.
            </p>
            <p>
             If you know some cities or parks you’d like to visit, maybe center your planning around those. You can see what’s around by visiting our
             <a href="/Destinations/Communities.aspx">
              cities map
             </a>
             or our
             <a href="/Destinations/Parks%20and%20Public%20Lands.aspx">
              parks map
             </a>
             .
            </p>

          <div class="container">
           <h2 class="content__header">
            Welcome to Alaska's Official Vacation Information Guide
           </h2>
           <div class="container grid-split">
            <div class="background background--slight">
             <p>
              As Governor of Alaska, I am pleased to welcome you to the Official State of Alaska vacation and travel information website. Alaska is different from every other destination in the world. Every day offers an unforgettable memory: a mother moose and calf, glaciers and mountains, unique Native cultures, our Russian legacy and Gold Rush days. Even lifelong Alaskans are amazed! And we have a wide range of accommodations and dining to suit every budget. Enjoy your online visit to Alaska, and I hope you'll come to visit the "Great Land" soon.
              <br/>
              <span class="link-block align-right">
               With warm regards,
               <br/>
               Bill Walker
              </span>
             </p>
            </div>
